        CASE WHEN ([Join2].[AdminUserId] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM   (SELECT TOP (2)

            FROM  [dbo].[T_AdminUserConfig] AS [Extent1]
            LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[T_Cities] AS [Extent2] ON [Extent1].[CityId] = [Extent2].[Id]
            WHERE (0 = [Extent1].[IsDeleted]) AND ([Extent1].[Id] = @p__linq__0) ) AS [Limit1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent3].[AdminUserId] AS [AdminUserId], [Extent4].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent4].[Name] AS [Name], [Extent4].[CreateDateTime] AS [CreateDateTime], [Extent4].[IsDeleted] AS [IsDeleted]
            FROM  [dbo].[T_AdminUserRoles] AS [Extent3]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[T_Roles] AS [Extent4] ON [Extent4].[Id] = [Extent3].[RoleId] ) AS [Join2] ON [Limit1].[Id] = [Join2].[AdminUserId]
    )  AS [Project2]
    ORDER BY [Project2].[Id] ASC, [Project2].[Id1] ASC, [Project2].[C1] ASC
